      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify">&#160;</div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">HUENENBERG, Switzerland &#8211; April 22,
2009 &#8211; </font>Alcon, Inc. (NYSE:ACL) reported global sales of $1,493.3 million
for the first quarter of 2009, a 4.8 percent increase excluding the impact of
foreign exchange fluctuations, or a decrease of 2.8 percent compared to the
first quarter of 2008 on a reported basis. Net earnings for the first quarter of
2009 increased 5.3 percent to $452.0 million compared to $429.4 million in the
first quarter of 2008.&#160;&#160;For the same periods, diluted earnings per
share increased 5.6 percent to $1.51 from $1.43.&#160;&#160;Excluding $13.1
million of after-tax costs associated with the company&#8217;s previously announced
restructuring program, both non-GAAP adjusted net earnings for the first quarter
of 2009 increased 8.3 percent to $465.1, and diluted earnings per share
increased 8.4 percent to $1.55 when compared to the first quarter of
2008.&#160;&#160;Reconciliations of reported and adjusted results for the first
quarter are included in the financial tables below.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;&#8220;Our global
diversification and commercial execution delivered organic sales growth in line
with our expectations and solid profit performance in spite of a challenging
global market environment,&#8221; said Kevin Buehler, Alcon&#8217;s president and chief
executive officer. &#8220;We will continue to manage discretionary costs in line with
the current market conditions while still investing in brand development and
research projects that will fuel future growth.&#8221;</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt"><br></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">First&#160;Quarter
Highlights</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">All
growth comparisons are for the first quarter of 2009 compared to the first
quarter of 2008.&#160;&#160;Organic sales growth rates provided below are
non-GAAP measures, which are reconciled in a table at the end of this
release.</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt; TEXT-ALIGN: center" align="justify">&#160;</div>

      sales achieved positive organic sales growth of 10.2 percent, but declined
      3.4 percent on a reported basis.&#160;&#160;Strong international
      pharmaceutical sales, especially in Japan, and a 14.1 percent organic
      sales growth rate, or a decline of 5.0 percent on a reported basis, for

      performance.</font></div>

      sales declined 2.1 percent&#160;due to generic competition to <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TOBRADEX<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font></font>

      organic increase, or a 4.8 decrease on a reported basis. <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Toric</font> and <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">AcrySof</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> ReSTOR</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font>&#160;<font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Aspheric</font> advanced

technologies.&#160;&#160;</font></div>

      decline in retailer inventories of contact lens solutions in the United
      States had a negative impact on sales of contact lens
      disinfectants.&#160;&#160;However, <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">OPTI</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">-</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">FREE</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> RepleniSH</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"> and EXPRESS</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>multipurpose
      disinfecting solutions maintained their position as the leading branded
      solutions on the market today.</font></div>
              </td>
            </tr>
        </table>
      </div>

                <div style="MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="justify"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">On
      March 10, the company announced a refractive laser contract with
      LCA-Vision for 75 <font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">ALLEGRETTO WAVE</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; FONT-SIZE: 70%; VERTICAL-ALIGN: super">&#174;</font><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</font>excimer
      lasers.&#160;&#160;The contract comes as part of a decision by LCA-Vision
      to standardize its laser surgery technology on two platforms based on

Year Outlook</font></div>
      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman"><font id="TAB2" style="LETTER-SPACING: 9pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;</font>&#160;Based on the
positive sales results for the first quarter of 2009, the company reaffirmed
that it expects to achieve its previously-issued, mid-single digit organic sales
growth target for 2009, which excludes currency fluctuations and
acquisitions.&#160;&#160;The company also reconfirmed that 2009 diluted earnings
per share on a U.S. GAAP basis are expected to be between $6.00 and $6.20 and
between $6.05 and $6.25 on a non-GAAP adjusted basis (excluding restructuring
charges).&#160;&#160;The company said its underlying performance and market
fundamentals support the achievement of full year guidance, with the recognition
that there will be some periodic variability in performance and such patterns
have been incorporated into expectations for the full year.</font></div>

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 13.7pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Alcon,

2008.&#160;Alcon, which has been dedicated to the ophthalmic industry for more
than&#160;60 years, researches, develops, manufactures and markets
pharmaceuticals, surgical equipment and devices, contact lens care solutions and
other vision care products that treat diseases, disorders and other conditions
of the eye.&#160;Alcon&#8217;s majority shareholder is Nestl&#233;, S.A., the world&#8217;s

of Alcon, Inc. For more information about Alcon, visit

      <div style="DISPLAY: block; MARGIN-LEFT: 0pt; TEXT-INDENT: 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 10.25pt; MARGIN-RIGHT: 0pt" align="left"><font style="DISPLAY: inline; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-FAMILY: Times New Roman">Note:
Organic change calculates sales growth without the impact of foreign exchange
fluctuations and acquisitions. Management believes organic sales change is an
important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it provides investors with
a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due to changes in unit
volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is considered a
non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated by the U.S.
Securities and Exchange Commission.&#160;&#160;Certain reclassifications have
been made to prior year amounts to conform with current year
presentation.</font><br>

Organic change&#160;presents&#160;sales growth without the impact of foreign
exchange fluctuations and acquisitions. Management believes organic sales
change&#160;is an important measure of the company&#8217;s operations because it
provides investors with a clearer picture of the core rate of sales growth due
to changes in unit volumes and local currency prices.&#160;&#160;This measure is
considered a non-GAAP financial measure as defined by Regulation G promulgated
by the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission.</font></div>
